# Canada Focus Tree

focus_tree = {
	id = canada_focus
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			tag = CAN
		}
	}
	default = no
	continuous_focus_position = { x = 3300 y = 1100 }

		}
